            document.getElementById('countryDistributionChart').innerHTML = 
                '<div class="has-text-centered p-6"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No data available</p></div>';
            document.getElementById('categoryDistributionChart').innerHTML = 
                '<div class="has-text-centered p-6"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No data available</p></div>';
                
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            // Process data and update charts as normal when portfolios are selected
        const heatmapData = calculateExposureData(selectedPortfolioIds, dimension);
            
            // Ensure we have valid data before rendering
            if (heatmapData && heatmapData.countries && heatmapData.countries.length > 0) {
        renderHeatmap(heatmapData, dimension);
            } else {
                // If no data available for the heatmap, show a message
                document.getElementById('riskHeatmap').innerHTML = 
                    '<div class="has-text-centered p-6">' +
                    '<p class="has-text-grey-light"><i class="fas fa-info-circle mr-2"></i>' +
                    'No data available for the selected portfolios and dimension.</p>' +
                    '</div>';
            }

        // Update doughnut charts
        const countryDistribution = calculateExposureByDimension(selectedPortfolioIds, 'country');
        const categoryDistribution = calculateExposureByDimension(selectedPortfolioIds, 'category');
        
            // Only render charts if we have data
            if (countryDistribution && countryDistribution.labels && countryDistribution.labels.length > 0) {
        renderDoughnutChart('countryDistributionChart', countryDistribution, 'Country Distribution');
            } else {
                document.getElementById('countryDistributionChart').innerHTML = 
                    '<div class="has-text-centered p-6"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No country data available</p></div>';
            }
            
            if (categoryDistribution && categoryDistribution.labels && categoryDistribution.labels.length > 0) {
        renderDoughnutChart('categoryDistributionChart', categoryDistribution, 'Category Distribution');
            } else {
                document.getElementById('categoryDistributionChart').innerHTML = 
                    '<div class="has-text-centered p-6"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No category data available</p></div>';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error updating risk breakdown:', error);
            // Show error message in the risk breakdown section
            document.getElementById('riskHeatmap').innerHTML = 
                '<div class="has-text-centered p-6">' +
                '<p class="has-text-grey-light"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-circle mr-2"></i>' +
                'An error occurred while updating the risk breakdown. Please try again.</p>' +
                '</div>';
        }
    }

    // Calculate exposure data for heatmap with intelligent filtering
    function calculateExposureData(selectedPortfolioIds, dimension) {
        const allCompanies = getAllCompaniesFromSelectedPortfolios();
        
        // Handle case where there are no companies (e.g., no portfolios selected)
        if (!allCompanies || allCompanies.length === 0) {
            console.log('No companies found for heat map calculation');
            return { 
                countries: [], 
                dims: [], 
                z: [],
                metadata: {
                    totalValue: 0,
                    countryPercentages: {},
                    dimensionPercentages: {}
                }
            };
        }
        
        const totalValue = allCompanies.reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.currentValue, 0);
        
        const exposure = {};
        const countryTotals = {}; // Track total per country for filtering
        const dimensionTotals = {}; // Track total per dimension for filtering
        
        // First pass: Collect all data points
        allCompanies.forEach(company => {
            // Handle unknown values gracefully
            const country = (company.country || '').trim() || 'Unknown';
            const dimValue = (company[dimension] || '').trim() || 'Unknown';
            
            // Initialize if needed
            if (!exposure[country]) exposure[country] = {};
            if (!exposure[country][dimValue]) exposure[country][dimValue] = 0;
            if (!countryTotals[country]) countryTotals[country] = 0;
            if (!dimensionTotals[dimValue]) dimensionTotals[dimValue] = 0;
            
            // Accumulate values
            const value = company.currentValue || 0;
            exposure[country][dimValue] += value;
            countryTotals[country] += value;
            dimensionTotals[dimValue] += value;
        });
        
        // Handle edge case: if no valid exposure data was collected
        if (Object.keys(exposure).length === 0) {
            console.log('No valid exposure data was collected');
            return { 
                countries: [], 
                dims: [], 
                z: [],
                metadata: {
                    totalValue: 0,
                    countryPercentages: {},
                    dimensionPercentages: {}
                }
            };
        }
        
        // Convert raw values to percentages
        for (const country in exposure) {
            for (const dim in exposure[country]) {
                exposure[country][dim] = totalValue > 0 ? 
                    (exposure[country][dim] / totalValue) * 100 : 0;
            }
        }
        
        // Calculate percentage thresholds for filtering
        const countryPercentages = {};
        const dimensionPercentages = {};
        
        for (const country in countryTotals) {
            countryPercentages[country] = totalValue > 0 ? 
                (countryTotals[country] / totalValue) * 100 : 0;
        }
        
        for (const dim in dimensionTotals) {
            dimensionPercentages[dim] = totalValue > 0 ? 
                (dimensionTotals[dim] / totalValue) * 100 : 0;
        }
        
        // Filter out insignificant countries and dimensions (< 1% of portfolio)
        // but always keep at least the top 8 of each
        const significanceThreshold = 1.0; // Min percentage to display by default
        
        // Sort countries and dimensions by percentage (descending)
        let sortedCountries = Object.entries(countryPercentages)
            .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
            .map(entry => entry[0]);
            
        let sortedDimensions = Object.entries(dimensionPercentages)
            .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
            .map(entry => entry[0]);
        
        // Filter but keep at least top 8 countries (or all if fewer than 8)
        const topCountryCount = Math.min(8, sortedCountries.length);
        const topCountries = sortedCountries.slice(0, topCountryCount);
        sortedCountries = sortedCountries.filter(country => 
            topCountries.includes(country) || countryPercentages[country] >= significanceThreshold
        );
        
        // Filter but keep at least top 8 dimensions (or all if fewer than 8)
        const topDimCount = Math.min(8, sortedDimensions.length);
        const topDimensions = sortedDimensions.slice(0, topDimCount);
        sortedDimensions = sortedDimensions.filter(dim => 
            topDimensions.includes(dim) || dimensionPercentages[dim] >= significanceThreshold
        );
        
        // Remap 'Unknown' to be last if present
        const moveUnknownToEnd = arr => {
            const idx = arr.indexOf('Unknown');
            if (idx !== -1) {
                arr.splice(idx, 1); 
                arr.push('Unknown');
            }
            return arr;
        };
        
        sortedCountries = moveUnknownToEnd(sortedCountries);
        sortedDimensions = moveUnknownToEnd(sortedDimensions);
        
        // Create z matrix for heatmap
        const z = sortedCountries.map(country => 
            sortedDimensions.map(dim => exposure[country]?.[dim] || 0)
        );
        
        // Return the optimized data for the heatmap
        return { 
            countries: sortedCountries, 
            dims: sortedDimensions, 
            z,
            // Additional metadata for tooltips
            metadata: {
                totalValue,
                countryPercentages,
                dimensionPercentages
            }
        };
    }

    function renderHeatmap(data, dimensionName) {
        // Enhanced error checking
        if (!data || !data.countries || !data.dims || 
            data.countries.length === 0 || data.dims.length === 0) {
            console.log('No data available for risk heatmap:', data);
            document.getElementById('riskHeatmap').innerHTML = 
                '<div class="has-text-centered p-4">' +
                '<p class="has-text-grey"><i class="fas fa-info-circle mr-2"></i>' +
                'No data available for the selected portfolios and dimension.</p>' +
                '</div>';
            return;
        }
        
        // Clean up any previous plot to avoid errors
        if (document.getElementById('riskHeatmap')) {
            Plotly.purge('riskHeatmap');
        }
        
        // Format dimension name for display
        const formattedDimensionName = dimensionName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + dimensionName.slice(1);
        
        // Truncate long labels for better display
        const truncateLabel = (label, maxLength = 15) => {
            if (label.length <= maxLength) return label;
            return label.substring(0, maxLength) + '...';
        };
        
        // Create shortened labels for display, but keep originals for tooltips
        const truncatedDims = data.dims.map(d => truncateLabel(d));
        const truncatedCountries = data.countries.map(c => truncateLabel(c));
        
        // Prepare custom data for enhanced tooltips using metadata
        const metadata = data.metadata || {};
        const customdata = data.countries.map((country, i) => 
            data.dims.map((dim, j) => ({
                country: country,
                dimension: dim,
                value: data.z[i][j],
                // Include overall allocations if available
                countryAllocation: metadata.countryPercentages?.[country] || 0,
                dimensionAllocation: metadata.dimensionPercentages?.[dim] || 0
            }))
        );
        
        // Generate a more visually appealing colorscale
        const colorscale = [
            [0, 'rgba(240, 240, 240, 0.6)'],    // Very light gray for 0 values
            [0.05, 'rgba(220, 238, 242, 0.9)'], // Very light bluish for small values
            [0.1, 'rgba(166, 216, 225, 1.0)'],  // Light blue
            [0.25, 'rgba(89, 164, 192, 1.0)'],  // Medium blue
            [0.5, 'rgba(33, 113, 181, 1.0)'],   // Dark blue
            [0.75, 'rgba(8, 69, 148, 1.0)'],    // Very dark blue
            [1.0, 'rgba(8, 48, 107, 1.0)']      // Deepest blue
        ];
        
        const trace = {
            type: 'heatmap',
            x: truncatedDims,
            y: truncatedCountries,
            z: data.z,
            colorscale: colorscale,
            showscale: true,
            hovertemplate: '<b>%{customdata.country}</b> × <b>%{customdata.dimension}</b><br>' +
                          'Cell Allocation: <b>%{z:.2f}%</b><br>' +
                          'Total Country Allocation: %{customdata.countryAllocation:.1f}%<br>' +
                          'Total ' + formattedDimensionName + ' Allocation: %{customdata.dimensionAllocation:.1f}%' +
                          '<extra></extra>',
            customdata: customdata
        };
        
        // Get the container dimensions for responsive sizing
        const container = document.getElementById('riskHeatmap');
        const containerWidth = container.offsetWidth;
        
        // Calculate a better height based on number of rows
        // More rows need more height to remain readable
        const baseHeight = 350;
        const rowCount = data.countries.length;
        const colCount = data.dims.length;
        let responsiveHeight;
        
        if (rowCount <= 5) {
            responsiveHeight = baseHeight;
        } else {
            // Add 20px per additional row beyond 5, with a max
            const additionalRows = Math.min(15, rowCount - 5); // Cap at 15 additional rows
            responsiveHeight = baseHeight + (additionalRows * 20);
        }
        
        // Calculate margins based on label lengths
        const longestCountryLabel = Math.max(...data.countries.map(c => c.length));
        const longestDimLabel = Math.max(...data.dims.map(d => d.length)); 
        
        // Adjust margins based on label length
        const leftMargin = Math.min(150, 60 + (longestCountryLabel * 4)); // 4px per character with a max
        const bottomMargin = Math.min(150, 50 + (longestDimLabel * 3)); // 3px per character with a max
        
        // Layout settings for the heatmap
        const layout = {
            title: '',
            showlegend: false,
            margin: {
                l: 50,
                r: 40,
                b: 50,
                t: 30,
                pad: 0
            },
            xaxis: {
                title: 'Volatility',
                tickfont: { size: 10 }
            },
            yaxis: {
                title: 'Return',
                tickfont: { size: 10 }
            }
        };
        
        // Use the centralized chart configuration
        Plotly.newPlot('riskHeatmap', [trace], layout, ChartConfig.plotlyConfig);
        
        // Force a resize after a short delay to ensure proper rendering
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (document.getElementById('riskHeatmap')) {
                Plotly.Plots.resize(document.getElementById('riskHeatmap'));
            }
        }, 100);
    }

    // Calculate exposure by a single dimension for bar charts
    function calculateExposureByDimension(selectedPortfolioIds, dimension) {
        try {
        const allCompanies = getAllCompaniesFromSelectedPortfolios();
            
            // Handle case when no portfolios are selected
            if (!allCompanies || allCompanies.length === 0) {
                console.log('No companies found for dimension exposure calculation');
                return { labels: [], values: [], percentages: [] };
            }
            
            const totalValue = allCompanies.reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.currentValue || 0), 0);
            
            // If total value is zero, return empty data structure
            if (totalValue <= 0) {
                console.log('Zero total value for dimension exposure calculation');
                return { labels: [], values: [], percentages: [] };
            }
        
        const exposure = {};
        
        allCompanies.forEach(company => {
                const dimValue = (company[dimension] || '').trim() || 'Unknown';
            if (!exposure[dimValue]) {
                exposure[dimValue] = 0;
            }
                exposure[dimValue] += company.currentValue || 0;
        });
        
        const exposureArray = Object.entries(exposure).map(([key, value]) => ({
            name: key,
                value: value, // Store actual monetary value
            percentage: totalValue > 0 ? (value / totalValue) * 100 : 0
        }));
        
        exposureArray.sort((a, b) => b.percentage - a.percentage);
        
            // Convert to format expected by renderDoughnutChart
            const labels = exposureArray.map(item => item.name);
            const values = exposureArray.map(item => item.value);
            const percentages = exposureArray.map(item => item.percentage);
            
            return { labels, values, percentages };
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error calculating exposure by dimension:', error);
            return { labels: [], values: [], percentages: [] };
        }
    }

    function renderBarChart(elementId, data, title) {
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            document.getElementById(elementId).innerHTML = 
                '<p class="has-text-centered">No data available</p>';
            return;
        }
        
        const labels = data.map(d => d.name);
        const values = data.map(d => d.percentage);
        
        const trace = {
            x: values,
            y: labels,
            type: 'bar',
            orientation: 'h',
            marker: {
                color: 'rgb(158,202,225)',
                opacity: 0.6,
                line: {
                    color: 'rgb(8,48,107)',
                    width: 1.5
                }
            }
        };
        
        const layout = {
            title: title,
            xaxis: { title: 'Percentage (%)' },
            yaxis: { title: '' },
            height: 400,
            margin: { l: 150, r: 50, t: 50, b: 50 },
            showlegend: false
        };
        
        Plotly.newPlot(elementId, [trace], layout, ChartConfig.plotlyConfig);
    }

    // Render doughnut charts
    function renderDoughnutChart(elementId, data, title) {
        try {
            // Handle both array format and object format with arrays
            if (!data) {
                console.log(`Cannot render doughnut chart: Data is null or undefined for ${elementId}`);
                document.getElementById(elementId).innerHTML = 
                    '<div class="has-text-centered p-4"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No data available</p></div>';
                return;
            }
            
            // Clear any previous chart to avoid errors
            if (document.getElementById(elementId)) {
                Plotly.purge(elementId);
            }
            
            // Check if data is in the new format (object with arrays)
            if (data.labels && Array.isArray(data.labels)) {
                // New format - directly use the arrays
                if (data.labels.length === 0) {
                    console.log(`Cannot render doughnut chart: Empty labels array for ${elementId}`);
                    document.getElementById(elementId).innerHTML = 
                        '<div class="has-text-centered p-4"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No data available</p></div>';
                    return;
                }
                
                const colors = generateColors(data.labels.length);
                
                // Create doughnut chart using PortfolioCharts utility
                PortfolioCharts.createDoughnutChart(
                    elementId,
                    data.labels,
                    data.values,
                    '',  // Empty title, since we have a subtitle already
                    colors,
                    data.percentages // Pass percentages for display purposes
                );
                
                return;
            }
            
            // Handle the old format (array of objects)
            if (!Array.isArray(data) || data.length === 0) {
                console.log(`Cannot render doughnut chart: Invalid data format for ${elementId}`);
                document.getElementById(elementId).innerHTML = 
                    '<div class="has-text-centered p-4"><p class="has-text-grey-light">No data available</p></div>';
            return;
        }
        
        // Prepare data for doughnut chart - take top 10 and group the rest as "Others"
        let labels = [];
        let values = [];
            let percentages = []; // For hover display
        
        if (data.length > 10) {
            // Take top 10 items
            const top10 = data.slice(0, 10);
            const others = data.slice(10);
            
            labels = top10.map(d => d.name);
                values = top10.map(d => d.value); // Use actual monetary values
                percentages = top10.map(d => d.percentage);
            
            // Add "Others" category
                const othersValue = others.reduce((sum, d) => sum + d.value, 0);
                const othersPercentage = others.reduce((sum, d) => sum + d.percentage, 0);
            if (othersValue > 0) {
                labels.push('Others');
                values.push(othersValue);
                    percentages.push(othersPercentage);
            }
        } else {
            labels = data.map(d => d.name);
                values = data.map(d => d.value); // Use actual monetary values
                percentages = data.map(d => d.percentage);
        }
        
        const colors = generateColors(labels.length);
        
        // Create doughnut chart using PortfolioCharts utility
        PortfolioCharts.createDoughnutChart(
            elementId,
            labels,
            values,
            '',  // Empty title, since we have a subtitle already
                colors,
                percentages // Pass percentages for display purposes
        );
        } catch (error) {
            console.error(`Error in renderDoughnutChart for ${elementId}:`, error);
            document.getElementById(elementId).innerHTML = 
                '<div class="has-text-centered p-4"><p class="has-text-grey-light">Error rendering chart</p></div>';
        }
    }
    
    // FIX: Initialize expandable sections for the Risk Breakdown using consistent event handling
    function initializeExpandableRiskSections() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-section .portfolio-header').forEach(header => {
            // Skip if we've already processed this header in renderPortfolioSections
            if (header.closest('.portfolio-section').dataset.portfolioId) {
                return;
            }
            
            const section = header.closest('.portfolio-section');
            
            // Add click handler using addEventListener for consistency
            header.addEventListener('click', function() {
                const content = section.querySelector('.portfolio-content');
                const icon = section.querySelector('.toggle-portfolio i');
                
                if (content.style.display === 'none') {
                    content.style.display = 'block';
                    icon.classList.remove('fa-chevron-down');
                    icon.classList.add('fa-chevron-up');
                    
                    // Ensure charts render correctly when expanding
                    window.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize'));
                    
                    // If this is the details section, make sure to render the charts
                    if (section.querySelector('#countryDistributionChart') || 
                        section.querySelector('#categoryDistributionChart')) {
                        const countryDistribution = calculateExposureByDimension(selectedPortfolioIds, 'country');
                        const categoryDistribution = calculateExposureByDimension(selectedPortfolioIds, 'category');
                        
                        renderDoughnutChart('countryDistributionChart', countryDistribution, 'Country Distribution');
                        renderDoughnutChart('categoryDistributionChart', categoryDistribution, 'Category Distribution');
                    }
                    
                    // If this is the heatmap section, make sure to render/resize the heatmap
                    if (section.querySelector('#riskHeatmap')) {
                        const dimension = document.getElementById('riskDimensionSelect').value;
                        const heatmapData = calculateExposureData(selectedPortfolioIds, dimension);
                        renderHeatmap(heatmapData, dimension);
                    }
                } else {
                    content.style.display = 'none';
                    icon.classList.remove('fa-chevron-up');
                    icon.classList.add('fa-chevron-down');
                }
            });
        });
    }

    // Add event listeners to toggle category companies
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        // Check if click was on or inside a toggle-companies element
        const toggleIcon = e.target.closest('.toggle-companies');
        if (!toggleIcon) return;
        
        const categoryName = toggleIcon.dataset.category;
        const portfolioId = toggleIcon.dataset.portfolioId;
        
        // Find the category row
        const categoryRow = toggleIcon.closest('.category-row');
        
        // Toggle icon
        const icon = toggleIcon.querySelector('i');
        const isExpanding = icon.classList.contains('fa-plus-circle');
        
        if (isExpanding) {
            icon.classList.remove('fa-plus-circle');
            icon.classList.add('fa-minus-circle');
            
            // Highlight the row when expanded
            categoryRow.classList.add('is-selected');
        } else {
            icon.classList.remove('fa-minus-circle');
            icon.classList.add('fa-plus-circle');
            
            // Remove highlight when collapsed
            categoryRow.classList.remove('is-selected');
        }
        
        // Toggle company rows with animation
        const companyRows = document.querySelectorAll(
            `.category-companies[data-parent-category="${categoryName}"][data-portfolio-id="${portfolioId}"]`
        );
        
        companyRows.forEach(row => {
            if (isExpanding) {
                // First make it visible but with 0 height
                row.classList.remove('is-hidden');
                row.style.maxHeight = '0';
                row.style.opacity = '0';
                
                // Force a reflow
                void row.offsetHeight;
                
                // Then animate to full height
                row.style.transition = 'max-height 0.3s ease, opacity 0.3s ease';
                row.style.maxHeight = '100px';
                row.style.opacity = '1';
            } else {
                // Animate to 0 height
                row.style.transition = 'max-height 0.3s ease, opacity 0.3s ease';
                row.style.maxHeight = '0';
                row.style.opacity = '0';
                
                // After animation, hide it
                setTimeout(() => {
                    row.classList.add('is-hidden');
                    row.style.maxHeight = '';
                    row.style.opacity = '';
                }, 300);
            }
        });
    });
});

// Add CSS for portfolio tabs and category rows
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Create style element
    const style = document.createElement('style');

<!-- Mobile Navigation JS -->
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // Functions to open and close a modal
    function openModal($el) {
        $el.classList.add('is-active');
    }

    function closeModal($el) {
        $el.classList.remove('is-active');
    }

    function closeAllModals() {
        (document.querySelectorAll('.modal') || []).forEach(($modal) => {
            closeModal($modal);
        });
    }

    // Add a click event on buttons to open a specific modal
    (document.querySelectorAll('.js-modal-trigger') || []).forEach(($trigger) => {
        const modal = $trigger.dataset.target;
        const $target = document.getElementById(modal);

        $trigger.addEventListener('click', () => {
            openModal($target);
        });
    });

    // Add a click event on various child elements to close the parent modal
    (document.querySelectorAll('.modal-background, .modal-close, .modal-card-head .delete, .modal-cancel') || []).forEach(($close) => {
        const $target = $close.closest('.modal');

        $close.addEventListener('click', () => {
            closeModal($target);
        });
    });

    // Navbar burger toggle
    const $navbarBurgers = Array.prototype.slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.navbar-burger'), 0);

    if ($navbarBurgers.length > 0) {
        $navbarBurgers.forEach(el => {
            el.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const target = el.dataset.target;
                const $target = document.getElementById(target);

                el.classList.toggle('is-active');
                $target.classList.toggle('is-active');
            });
        });
    }
});
</script>

<script>
    // Auto-dismiss notifications after 5 seconds
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        const notifications = document.querySelectorAll('.message-notification');
        
        notifications.forEach(notification => {
            // Add click event for delete button
            const deleteButton = notification.querySelector('.delete');
            if (deleteButton) {
                deleteButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    notification.remove();
                });
            }
            
            // Auto-dismiss after 5 seconds
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.classList.add('is-fading-out');
                
                // Remove element after fade-out animation (0.5s)
                setTimeout(() => {
                    notification.remove();
                }, 500);
            }, 5000);
        });
    });
</script>

###START_FILE_PATH: templates/components/analyse_components.html###
<!-- analyse_components.html -->
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8">
  <title>Portfolio Analysis Chart Components</title>
  <!-- Plotly.js is already included in base.html -->
  <style>
    .sunburst-legend {
      max-height: 150px;
      overflow-y: auto;
    }
    .legend-item.highlighted {
      font-weight: bold;
      text-decoration: underline;
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>

<script>
/**
 * NOTE:
 * -------
 * This version assumes that the following global variables
 * are set from your main "analyse.html" script:
 *
 *   window.portfolioData
 *   window.formatCurrency
 *   window.formatPercentage
 *   window.generateColors
 *
 * The "Companies" doughnut chart code already lives in "analyse.html"
 * where these variables exist. For the "Categories" sunburst chart
 * to work, the code below references them via window.* (or expects
 * them to be in global scope).
 *
 * The key fix is that the "Categories" tab logic no longer tries
 * to use a local 'portfolioData' that doesn't exist, and instead
 * calls window.portfolioData. Also, we remove repeated references
 * to format functions as parameters, and just read them from
 * window.formatCurrency, etc.
 */

window.PortfolioCharts = (function() {
    /**
     * Creates a doughnut (pie) chart with a hole in the middle.
     * @param {string} elementId - ID of the element to render chart in
     * @param {Array<string>} labels - Array of labels
     * @param {Array<number>} values - Array of actual monetary values
     * @param {string} title - Chart title
     * @param {Array<string>} colors - Array of colors
     * @param {Array<number>} percentages - Optional array of percentages for display
     */
    function createDoughnutChart(elementId, labels, values, title, colors, percentages) {
        // Use the globally defined formatCurrency:
        const formatCurrency = window.formatCurrency || (v => v);

        // Use the centralized chart configuration
        return ChartConfig.createDoughnutChart(elementId, labels, values, {
            title: title,
            colors: colors,
            percentages: percentages,
            formatCurrency: formatCurrency,
            formatPercentage: window.formatPercentage || (v => v),
            height: 400
        });
    }

    /**
     * Creates a sunburst chart for category breakdowns.
     */
    function createSunburstChart(elementId, portfolio, formatCurrencyParam, formatPercentageParam, generateColorsParam) {
        // Use provided parameters or fall back to window globals
        const formatCurrency    = formatCurrencyParam || window.formatCurrency    || (v => v);
        const formatPercentage  = formatPercentageParam || window.formatPercentage  || (v => v);
        const generateColors    = generateColorsParam || window.generateColors    || (count => []);

        const categories = portfolio.categories || [];
        console.log(`Creating sunburst chart for ${elementId} with ${categories.length} categories`);
        
        // Prepare the chart container
        const chartContainer = prepareChartContainer(elementId);
        if (!chartContainer) {
            console.error(`Chart container element not found: ${elementId}`);
            return null;
        }
        
        if (categories.length === 0) {
            chartContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="has-text-centered p-6">No category data available</div>';
            return null;
        }
        
        // Special handling for single category case (often just "Uncategorized")
        if (categories.length === 1 && categories[0].name === "Uncategorized") {
            console.log(`Portfolio ${portfolio.id} has only a single "Uncategorized" category with ${categories[0].companies.length} companies`);
            
            // If there are no companies in this category, show a message
            if (categories[0].companies.length === 0) {
                chartContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="has-text-centered p-6">No categorized data available</div>';
                return null;
            }
            
            // Log the companies for debugging
            categories[0].companies.forEach(company => {
                console.log(`  - ${company.name}: ${company.currentValue} (${company.percentage}%)`);
            });
        }
        
        // Ensure the chart container is fully visible and sized
        // This is critical for Plotly to render correctly
        chartContainer.style.display = 'block';
        chartContainer.style.height = '450px';
        chartContainer.style.width = '100%';
        chartContainer.style.position = 'relative';
        chartContainer.style.visibility = 'visible';
        chartContainer.style.opacity = '1';
        chartContainer.style.minHeight = '400px';
        chartContainer.style.minWidth = '300px';
        
        // Force a reflow to ensure dimensions are applied
        void chartContainer.offsetHeight;
        
        // Build arrays with categories as top-level nodes
        const labels = [];
        const parents = [];
        const values = [];
        const colors = [];
        const text = [];
        const ids = [];
        
        // Get colors using window.generateColors or fallback to a local implementation
        let categoryColors;
        if (typeof window.generateColors === 'function') {
            categoryColors = window.generateColors(categories.length);
            console.log('Using global generateColors function');
        } else {
            console.warn('Global generateColors function not found, using fallback');
            // Fallback color generation
            categoryColors = [];
            const defaultColors = [
                '#3366CC', '#DC3912', '#FF9900', '#109618', '#990099', '#3B3EAC',
                '#0099C6', '#DD4477', '#66AA00', '#B82E2E', '#316395', '#994499'
            ];
            
            for (let i = 0; i < categories.length; i++) {
                categoryColors.push(defaultColors[i % defaultColors.length]);
            }
        }
        
        console.log('Generated category colors:', categoryColors);
        
        // Top-level category nodes
        categories.forEach((category, index) => {
            // Add percentage to the label for top-level categories
            labels.push(`${category.name} (${formatPercentage(category.percentage)})`);
            parents.push(""); // top-level has no parent
            values.push(category.currentValue);
            ids.push(`category-${category.name}`);
            text.push(
                `<b>${formatPercentage(category.percentage)}</b><br>${formatCurrency(category.currentValue)}`
            );
            colors.push(categoryColors[index]);
        });
        
        // Company (child) nodes
        categories.forEach((category, index) => {
            const categoryName = category.name;
            const categoryColor = categoryColors[index];
            category.companies.forEach(company => {
                // Add percentage to the company label
                labels.push(`${company.name} (${formatPercentage(company.percentage)})`);
                parents.push(`category-${categoryName}`);
                values.push(company.currentValue);
                ids.push(`company-${company.name}`);
                const companyText =
                    `<b>${formatPercentage(company.percentage)}</b> of portfolio<br>` +
                    `<b>${formatPercentage(company.categoryPercentage)}</b> of ${categoryName}<br>` +
                    `${formatCurrency(company.currentValue)}`;
                text.push(companyText);
                
                // Use a lighter color for sub-nodes
                const lighterColor = adjustColorBrightness(categoryColor, 30);
                colors.push(lighterColor);
            });
        });
        
        // Log data for debugging
        console.log(`Chart data prepared: ${labels.length} labels, ${parents.length} parents, ${values.length} values`);
        
        // Special handling for single category with "Uncategorized"
        // Make sure we have enough data to create a meaningful chart
        if (labels.length < 3) {
            console.warn(`Not enough data points for a meaningful sunburst chart (${labels.length})`);
            
            // If it's just a single "Uncategorized" category, create a simpler pie chart instead
            if (categories.length === 1 && categories[0].name === "Uncategorized" && categories[0].companies.length > 0) {
                console.log("Creating pie chart for single Uncategorized category");
                
                // Create a simpler pie chart with just the companies
                const companyLabels = categories[0].companies.map(c => `${c.name} (${formatPercentage(c.percentage)})`);
                const companyValues = categories[0].companies.map(c => c.currentValue);
                const companyColors = generateColors(companyLabels.length);
                
                const pieData = [{
                    type: 'pie',
                    labels: companyLabels,
                    values: companyValues,
                    textinfo: 'label+percent',
                    hovertemplate: '<b>%{label}</b><br>%{value:,.2f} (%{percent})<extra></extra>',
                    marker: { colors: companyColors }
                }];
                
                const pieLayout = {
                    title: 'Companies (Uncategorized)',
                    height: 450,
                    margin: { l: 20, r: 20, t: 50, b: 20 },
                    showlegend: false
                };
                
                // Use the centralized configuration
                return Plotly.newPlot(elementId, pieData, pieLayout, ChartConfig.plotlyConfig);
            }
        }
        
        const data = [{
            type: 'sunburst',
            labels: labels,
            parents: parents,
            values: values,
            ids: ids,
            text: text,
            textinfo: 'label',
            insidetextorientation: 'radial',
            hovertemplate: '<b>%{label}</b><br>%{text}<extra></extra>',
            branchvalues: 'total',
            marker: { colors: colors, line: { width: 1, color: 'white' } },
            sort: false
        }];
        
        const layout = {
            margin: { l: 0, r: 0, t: 0, b: 0 },
            height: 450,
            width: chartContainer.offsetWidth || 500,
            autosize: true
        };
        
        console.log(`Creating sunburst with dimensions: ${layout.width}x${layout.height}`);
        
        // Use the centralized configuration
        const config = ChartConfig.plotlyConfig;
        
        try {
            // Create the plot
            Plotly.newPlot(elementId, data, layout, config)
                .then(() => {
                    console.log(`Sunburst chart ${elementId} created successfully`);
                    
                    // Ensure the chart is still visible after a short delay
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        const element = document.getElementById(elementId);
                        if (element) {
                            element.style.visibility = 'visible';
                            element.style.opacity = '1';
                            Plotly.Plots.resize(element);
                        }
                    }, 200);
                })
                .catch(error => {
                    console.error(`Error in Plotly.newPlot for ${elementId}:`, error);
                });
        } catch (plotlyError) {
            console.error(`Exception in Plotly.newPlot for ${elementId}:`, plotlyError);
        }
        
        return chartContainer;
    }

    /**
     * Adds a clickable legend for the sunburst chart.
     */
    function addSunburstLegend(portfolio, categories, categoryColors, formatPercentage, chartElementId) {
        const formatPct = window.formatPercentage || (v => v);

        let legendContainer = document.getElementById(`categoryLegend${portfolio.id}`);
        if (!legendContainer) {
            const chartContainer = document.getElementById(chartElementId).parentNode;
            legendContainer = document.createElement('div');
            legendContainer.id = `categoryLegend${portfolio.id}`;
            legendContainer.className = 'sunburst-legend mt-3';
            chartContainer.after(legendContainer);
        }
        legendContainer.innerHTML = '';
        
        // Legend title removed as requested
        
        const legendGrid = document.createElement('div');
        legendGrid.className = 'legend-grid is-flex is-flex-wrap-wrap is-justify-content-center';
        
        categories.forEach((category, index) => {
            const color = categoryColors[index];
            const legendItem = document.createElement('div');
            legendItem.className = 'legend-item is-flex is-align-items-center mr-3 mb-2';
            legendItem.style.cursor = 'pointer';
            legendItem.innerHTML = `
                <span class="color-box mr-1" style="background-color: ${color}; width: 12px; height: 12px; display: inline-block;"></span>
                <span class="is-size-7">${category.name} (${formatPct(category.percentage)})</span>
            `;
            
            legendItem.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const chart = document.getElementById(chartElementId);
                if (legendItem.classList.contains('highlighted')) {
                    Plotly.restyle(chart, { 'level': [undefined], 'root': [null] });
                    legendItem.classList.remove('highlighted');
                } else {
                    Plotly.restyle(chart, { 'level': [2] });
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        Plotly.restyle(chart, { 'root': [`category-${category.name}`] });
                    }, 10);
                    document.querySelectorAll(`#categoryLegend${portfolio.id} .legend-item`)
                            .forEach(item => item.classList.remove('highlighted'));
                    legendItem.classList.add('highlighted');
                }
            });
            
            legendGrid.appendChild(legendItem);
        });
        
        legendContainer.appendChild(legendGrid);
        
        // Reset button
        const resetButton = document.createElement('button');
        resetButton.className = 'button is-small is-light mt-2';
        resetButton.innerText = 'Reset View';
        resetButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const chart = document.getElementById(chartElementId);
            Plotly.restyle(chart, { 'level': [undefined], 'root': [null] });
            document.querySelectorAll(`#categoryLegend${portfolio.id} .legend-item`)
                    .forEach(item => item.classList.remove('highlighted'));
        });
        
        const buttonContainer = document.createElement('div');
        buttonContainer.className = 'has-text-centered';
        buttonContainer.appendChild(resetButton);
        legendContainer.appendChild(buttonContainer);
    }

    /**
     * Brighten or darken a given hex color by 'percent' (positive or negative).
     * Includes error handling for undefined or invalid hex values.
     */
    function adjustColorBrightness(hex, percent) {
        // Default color if hex is undefined or invalid
        if (!hex || typeof hex !== 'string' || !hex.startsWith('#') || hex.length !== 7) {
            console.warn(`Invalid hex color provided to adjustColorBrightness: ${hex}`);
            return '#CCCCCC'; // Return a neutral gray as fallback
        }
        
        try {
            let r = parseInt(hex.substr(1, 2), 16);
            let g = parseInt(hex.substr(3, 2), 16);
            let b = parseInt(hex.substr(5, 2), 16);
            
            // Check if parsing was successful
            if (isNaN(r) || isNaN(g) || isNaN(b)) {
                console.warn(`Failed to parse hex color: ${hex}`);
                return '#CCCCCC';
            }
            
            r = Math.min(255, Math.max(0, r + percent));
            g = Math.min(255, Math.max(0, g + percent));
            b = Math.min(255, Math.max(0, b + percent));
            return '#' + ((1 << 24) + (r << 16) + (g << 8) + b).toString(16).slice(1);
        } catch (error) {
            console.error(`Error in adjustColorBrightness: ${error.message}`);
            return '#CCCCCC';
        }
    }

    /**
     * Updates an existing doughnut chart with new data.
     */
    function updateDoughnutChart(elementId, labels, values, colors) {
        ChartConfig.updateDoughnutChart(elementId, labels, values, colors);
    }

    /**
     * Resizes Plotly charts whenever the window is resized,
     * specifically focusing on the active "Categories" tab charts.
     */
    function setupResizeHandlers() {
        window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
            // For each active categories tab, relayout
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-pane.is-active [id^="categoryChart"]').forEach(element => {
                Plotly.Plots.resize(element);
            });
            // Also resize global charts if present
            if (document.getElementById('portfolioAllocationsChart')) {
                Plotly.Plots.resize(document.getElementById('portfolioAllocationsChart'));
            }
            if (document.getElementById('companyAllocationsChart')) {
                Plotly.Plots.resize(document.getElementById('companyAllocationsChart'));
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * Enhances the existing tab initialization so that when a "Categories" tab
     * is clicked, we attempt to create (or recreate) the sunburst chart.
     */
    function setupTabChangeHandlers(initializePortfolioTabs) {
        const enhancedInitTabs = function() {
            // Call the original tab init
            initializePortfolioTabs();

            // For each tab that references categories
            document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-section .tabs li[data-tab*="categories"]').forEach(tab => {
                const originalHandler = tab.onclick;
                tab.onclick = function(e) {
                    // First run any existing click handler
                    if (originalHandler) {
                        originalHandler.call(this, e);
                    }
                    const tabId = this.getAttribute('data-tab');
                    const portfolioId = tabId.split('-')[1];
                    console.log(`Tab switched to categories for portfolio ${portfolioId}`);
                    
                    /**
                     * Repeated attempts to create the sunburst chart, ensuring
                     * the container is actually visible with a non-zero size.
                     */
                    function createCategoryChart(attempt = 1) {
                        console.log(`Chart creation attempt ${attempt} for portfolio ${portfolioId}`);
                        const elementId = `categoryChart${portfolioId}`;
                        const chartElement = prepareChartContainer(elementId);
                        if (!chartElement) {
                            console.error(`Chart element not found: ${elementId}`);
                            return;
                        }
                        
                        // If container is not visible, retry up to 5 times
                        const isVisible = chartElement.offsetParent !== null && chartElement.offsetWidth > 0;
                        console.log(`Chart container visible: ${isVisible}, width: ${chartElement.offsetWidth}, height: ${chartElement.offsetHeight}`);
                        
                        if (!isVisible && attempt < 5) {
                            const tabPane = chartElement.closest('.tab-pane');
                            if (tabPane) {
                                tabPane.style.display = 'block';
                                tabPane.style.visibility = 'visible';
                                tabPane.style.opacity = '1';
                                tabPane.classList.add('is-active');
                            }
                            
                            // Ensure the chart container itself is visible
                            chartElement.style.display = 'block';
                            chartElement.style.visibility = 'visible';
                            chartElement.style.opacity = '1';
                            chartElement.style.height = '450px';
                            chartElement.style.width = '100%';
                            chartElement.style.minHeight = '400px';
                            chartElement.style.minWidth = '300px';
                            
                            // Force a reflow
                            void chartElement.offsetHeight;
                            
                            setTimeout(() => createCategoryChart(attempt + 1), 100 * attempt);
                            return;
                        }
                        
                        // Now retrieve the correct portfolio from the global data
                        let portfolio;
                        let portfolioName = null;
                        
                        // Get the portfolio name from the tab text
                        const tabsContainer = tab.closest('.tabs');
                        if (tabsContainer) {
                            const portfolioHeader = tabsContainer.closest('.portfolio-section').querySelector('h2');
                            if (portfolioHeader) {
                                portfolioName = portfolioHeader.textContent.trim();
                                console.log(`Tab for portfolio name: ${portfolioName}`);
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // First try to find it by ID in window.portfolioData array
                        if (Array.isArray(window.portfolioData)) {
                            portfolio = window.portfolioData.find(p => p.id == portfolioId);
                            
                            // If not found by ID, try by name as fallback
                            if (!portfolio && portfolioName) {
                                portfolio = window.portfolioData.find(p => p.name === portfolioName);
                                console.log(`Found portfolio by name: ${portfolioName} instead of ID ${portfolioId}`);
                                
                                // If still not found, try case-insensitive match
                                if (!portfolio) {
                                    const lowerName = portfolioName.toLowerCase();
                                    portfolio = window.portfolioData.find(p => p.name.toLowerCase() === lowerName);
                                    if (portfolio) {
                                        console.log(`Found portfolio by case-insensitive name: ${portfolioName}`);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        // Then check if it's in window.portfolioData object by ID
                        else if (window.portfolioData && window.portfolioData[portfolioId]) {
                            portfolio = window.portfolioData[portfolioId];
                        }
                        // If still not found but we have portfolio data and name, find by name
                        else if (window.portfolioData && portfolioName) {
                            // Check all portfolios in the object to find by name
                            for (const key in window.portfolioData) {
                                if (window.portfolioData[key].name === portfolioName) {
                                    portfolio = window.portfolioData[key];
                                    console.log(`Found portfolio in object by name: ${portfolioName}`);
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        
                        if (!portfolio) {
                            console.error(`Portfolio data not found for ID ${portfolioId} or name ${portfolioName}`);
                            console.log('Available portfolios:', window.portfolioData);
                            
                            // Add a message in the chart container
                            const elementId = `categoryChart${portfolioId}`;
                            const chartElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                            if (chartElement) {
                                chartElement.innerHTML = `
                                    <div class="has-text-centered p-6">
                                        <p class="has-text-danger">Portfolio data not found</p>
                                        <p>Unable to find portfolio with ID: ${portfolioId}</p>
                                        <p>Please refresh the page or contact support if this issue persists.</p>
                                    </div>
                                `;
                            }
                            return;
                        }
                        
                        try {
                            // Create or re-create the sunburst with all parameters
                            PortfolioCharts.createSunburstChart(
                                elementId, 
                                portfolio, 
                                window.formatCurrency, 
                                window.formatPercentage, 
                                window.generateColors
                            );
                            
                            // Check if the chart actually rendered and retry if needed
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                if (!chartElement.querySelector('.main-svg') && attempt < 5) {
                                    console.log('Chart not rendered properly, trying again...');
                                    createCategoryChart(attempt + 1);
                                } else {
                                    // Ensure the chart is properly sized
                                    Plotly.Plots.resize(chartElement);
                                    window.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize'));
                                    
                                    // Add another check after a delay to ensure it stays visible
                                    setTimeout(() => {
                                        if (chartElement.offsetWidth === 0 || chartElement.offsetHeight === 0 ||
                                            chartElement.style.visibility === 'hidden' || chartElement.style.opacity === '0') {
                                            console.log('Chart disappeared after rendering, restoring...');
                                            chartElement.style.display = 'block';
                                            chartElement.style.visibility = 'visible';
                                            chartElement.style.opacity = '1';
                                            Plotly.Plots.resize(chartElement);
                                        }
                                    }, 500);
                                }
                            }, 100);
                        } catch (error) {
                            console.error(`Error creating chart: ${error}`, error.stack);
                            chartElement.innerHTML = `
                                <div class="has-text-centered p-6">
                                    <p class="has-text-danger">Error loading chart</p>
                                    <button class="button is-small is-info mt-2" onclick="window.createCategoryChart(${portfolioId})">
                                        Retry
                                    </button>
                                </div>
                            `;
                            // Expose a retry function on window
                            window.createCategoryChart = function(id) {
                                console.log(`Manual retry for chart ${id}`);
                                const portfolioSection = document.querySelector(`.portfolio-section[data-portfolio-id="${id}"]`);
                                if (portfolioSection) {
                                    const categoriesTab = portfolioSection.querySelector('.tabs li[data-tab*="categories"]');
                                    if (categoriesTab) {
                                        categoriesTab.click();
                                    }
                                }
                            };
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Delay a bit to let the DOM update
                    setTimeout(createCategoryChart, 300);
                };
            });
        };
        return enhancedInitTabs;
    }

    return {
        createDoughnutChart: createDoughnutChart,
        createSunburstChart: createSunburstChart,
        updateDoughnutChart: updateDoughnutChart,
        setupResizeHandlers: setupResizeHandlers,
        setupTabChangeHandlers: setupTabChangeHandlers,
        adjustColorBrightness: adjustColorBrightness
    };
})();

/**
 * Ensures the chart container is fully visible with
 * consistent styling. Returns the container element
 * or null if not found.
 */
function prepareChartContainer(elementId) {
    const chartElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
    if (!chartElement) {
        console.error(`Chart element not found: ${elementId}`);
        return null;
    }
    
    // Force the parent column to be visible/flex
    const chartColumn = chartElement.closest('.column');
    if (chartColumn) {
        chartColumn.style.display = 'flex';
        chartColumn.style.visibility = 'visible';
        chartColumn.style.opacity = '1';
        // Ensure the column has minimum dimensions
        chartColumn.style.minHeight = '450px';
        chartColumn.style.minWidth = '300px';
    }
    
    // Also ensure any parent containers are visible
    const chartContainer = chartElement.closest('.chart-medium-container');
    if (chartContainer) {
        chartContainer.style.display = 'flex';
        chartContainer.style.visibility = 'visible';
        chartContainer.style.opacity = '1';
        chartContainer.style.height = '100%';
        chartContainer.style.width = '100%';
    }
    
    // Clear any previous content
    chartElement.innerHTML = '';
    chartElement.style.display = 'block';
    chartElement.style.height = '450px';
    chartElement.style.width = '100%';
    chartElement.style.position = 'relative';
    chartElement.style.visibility = 'visible';
    chartElement.style.opacity = '1';
    chartElement.style.zIndex = '1';
    
    // Add explicit min dimensions to prevent zero-size issues
    chartElement.style.minHeight = '400px';
    chartElement.style.minWidth = '300px';
    
    // Force a reflow to ensure styles are applied
    void chartElement.offsetHeight;
    
    // Log the final dimensions
    console.log(`Chart container ${elementId} dimensions: ${chartElement.offsetWidth}x${chartElement.offsetHeight}`);
    
    return chartElement;
}

/**
 * Enhances the existing sunburst creation so we can
 * handle zero-width containers by forcibly giving them
 * default dimensions before building the chart.
 */
function enhanceSunburstChart() {
    const originalCreateSunburst = PortfolioCharts.createSunburstChart;
    PortfolioCharts.createSunburstChart = function(elementId, portfolio, formatCurrency, formatPercentage, generateColors) {
        const chartContainer = document.getElementById(elementId);
        if (!chartContainer) {
            console.error(`Chart container not found: ${elementId}`);
            return null;
        }
        console.log(`Creating sunburst in container with dimensions: ${chartContainer.offsetWidth}x${chartContainer.offsetHeight}`);
        if (chartContainer.offsetWidth === 0) {
            console.warn('Chart container has zero width, setting default width');
            chartContainer.style.width = '100%';
            chartContainer.style.minWidth = '400px';
        }
        if (chartContainer.offsetHeight === 0) {
            console.warn('Chart container has zero height, setting default height');
            chartContainer.style.height = '450px';
            chartContainer.style.minHeight = '400px';
        }
        // Force a reflow to ensure dimensions are applied
        void chartContainer.offsetHeight;
        // Pass all parameters to the original function
        return originalCreateSunburst(elementId, portfolio, formatCurrency, formatPercentage, generateColors);
    };
    return PortfolioCharts;
}

/**
 * Forces a chart redraw when a portfolio is toggled open
 * and the "Categories" tab is already active.
 */
function enhancePortfolioToggle() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-section .portfolio-header').forEach(header => {
        const originalHandler = header.onclick;
        header.onclick = function(e) {
            if (originalHandler) {
                originalHandler.call(this, e);
            }
            const section = this.closest('.portfolio-section');
            const content = section.querySelector('.portfolio-content');
            if (content && content.style.display === 'block') {
                const activeTab = section.querySelector('.tabs li.is-active');
                if (activeTab && activeTab.getAttribute('data-tab').includes('categories')) {
                    console.log('Portfolio expanded with categories tab active - triggering chart redraw');
                    setTimeout(() => activeTab.click(), 300);
                }
            }
        };
    });
}

/**
 * Ensures all sunburst charts remain visible by periodically checking
 * and restoring their visibility if needed.
 */
function ensureChartsRemainVisible() {
    // Check all category charts every 500ms
    setInterval(() => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[id^="categoryChart"]').forEach(chart => {
            if (chart.offsetParent !== null) { // Only check visible charts
                // If the chart is visible but has zero dimensions or is hidden
                if (chart.offsetWidth === 0 || chart.offsetHeight === 0 || 
                    chart.style.visibility === 'hidden' || chart.style.opacity === '0') {
                    
                    console.log(`Restoring visibility for chart ${chart.id}`);
                    
                    // Restore visibility and dimensions
                    chart.style.display = 'block';
                    chart.style.visibility = 'visible';
                    chart.style.opacity = '1';
                    chart.style.height = '450px';
                    chart.style.width = '100%';
                    chart.style.minHeight = '400px';
                    chart.style.minWidth = '300px';
                    
                    // Force a reflow
                    void chart.offsetHeight;
                    
                    // Resize the chart
                    try {
                        Plotly.Plots.resize(chart);
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.warn(`Error resizing chart ${chart.id}:`, e);
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }, 500);
}

/**
 * When the DOM is ready, enhance the sunburst creation
 * and set up toggles for portfolio expansions.
 */
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Patch the sunburst creation to handle zero-size containers
    PortfolioCharts = enhanceSunburstChart();

    // Re-run the categories chart if a portfolio is toggled open
    setTimeout(enhancePortfolioToggle, 1000);

    // Also attempt to redraw if the entire window is resized
    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-section').forEach(section => {
            const content = section.querySelector('.portfolio-content');
            if (content && content.style.display === 'block') {
                const activeTab = section.querySelector('.tabs li.is-active');
                if (activeTab && activeTab.getAttribute('data-tab').includes('categories')) {
                    const portfolioId = section.dataset.portfolioId;
                    console.log(`Resizing triggered redraw for portfolio ${portfolioId}`);
                    setTimeout(() => activeTab.click(), 200);
                }
            }
        });
    });
    
    // Start the visibility check
    ensureChartsRemainVisible();
});
</script>

</body>
</html>

                                            </span>
                                        </th>

                                            Category

                                                <i :class="sortDirection === 'asc' ? 'fas fa-sort-up' : 'fas fa-sort-down'"></i>
                                            </span>
                                        </th>
                                        <th @click="sortBy('shares')" class="is-sortable">
                                            Shares
                                            <span class="icon is-small ml-1" v-if="sortColumn === 'shares'">
                                                <i :class="sortDirection === 'asc' ? 'fas fa-sort-up' : 'fas fa-sort-down'"></i>
                                            </span>
                                        </th>
                                        <th @click="sortBy('price_eur')" class="is-sortable">
                                            Price (EUR)
                                            <span class="icon is-small ml-1" v-if="sortColumn === 'price_eur'">
                                                <i :class="sortDirection === 'asc' ? 'fas fa-sort-up' : 'fas fa-sort-down'"></i>
                                            </span>
                                        </th>
                                        <th @click="sortBy('total_value')" class="is-sortable">
                                            Total Value
                                            <span class="icon is-small ml-1" v-if="sortColumn === 'total_value'">
                                                <i :class="sortDirection === 'asc' ? 'fas fa-sort-up' : 'fas fa-sort-down'"></i>
                                            </span>
                                        </th>

                                            Total Invested
                                            <span class="icon is-small ml-1" v-if="sortColumn === 'total_invested'">
                                                <i :class="sortDirection === 'asc' ? 'fas fa-sort-up' : 'fas fa-sort-down'"></i>
                                            </span>
                                        </th>
                                        <th @click="sortBy('last_updated')" class="is-sortable">
                                            Last Update
                                            <span class="icon is-small ml-1" v-if="sortColumn === 'last_updated'">
                                                <i :class="sortDirection === 'asc' ? 'fas fa-sort-up' : 'fas fa-sort-down'"></i>
                                            </span>
                                        </th>
                                        <th>Actions</th>
                                    </tr>
                                </thead>
                                <tbody>
                                    <tr v-for="item in filteredPortfolioItems" :key="item.id">
                                        <td>
                                            <button 
                                                class="button is-small is-info" 
                                                @click="confirmPriceUpdate(item)"
                                                :class="{'is-loading': isUpdating && selectedItem.id === item.id}"
                                                :disabled="isUpdating"
                                                title="Update price immediately">
                                                <span class="icon is-small">
                                                    <i class="fas fa-sync"></i>
                                                </span>
                                            </button>

                                        <td>
                                            <input class="input is-small" type="text"
                                                   v-model="item.identifier"

                                        <td>

                                        </td>
                                        <td class="input-column">

                                                        @change="debouncedSavePortfolioChange(item)">

                                                    {% for portfolio in portfolios %}
                                                        <option value="{{ portfolio }}">{{ portfolio }}</option>
                                                    {% endfor %}
                                                </select>
                                            </div>
                                        </td>
                                        <td class="input-column">
                                            <input class="input is-small" type="text"
                                                   v-model="item.category"
                                                   @input="debouncedSaveCategoryChange(item)"
                                                   @change="saveCategoryChange(item)">
                                        </td>
                                        <td class="input-column">
                                            <input class="input is-small" type="text"
                                                   :value="formatNumber(item.shares)"
                                                   @input="(e) => { item.shares = parseFloat(e.target.value); debouncedSaveSharesChange(item); }"
                                                   @change="saveSharesChange(item)">
                                        </td>
                                        <td :class="{'has-text-danger': !item.price_eur}">
                                            <span v-text="item.price_eur ? formatCurrency(item.price_eur) : 'No price'"></span>
                                        </td>
                                        <td>
                                            <span v-text="formatCurrency(item.price_eur * item.shares)"></span>
                                        </td>
                                        <td>
                                            <span v-text="formatCurrency(item.total_invested)"></span>
                                        </td>
                                        <td>
                                            <span v-text="formatDateAgo(item.last_updated)"></span>
                                        </td>
                                        <td>
                                            <div class="buttons is-right">
                                                <button 
                                                    class="button is-small is-danger" 
                                                    @click="confirmDelete(item)"
                                                    :class="{'is-loading': isDeleting && selectedItem.id === item.id}"
                                                    :disabled="isDeleting">
                                                    <span class="icon is-small">
                                                        <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
                                                    </span>
                                                </button>
                                            </div>
                                        </td>
                                    </tr>
                                </tbody>
                            </table>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <!-- Delete Confirmation Modal -->
                    <div class="modal" :class="{'is-active': showDeleteModal}">
                        <div class="modal-background" @click="closeModal"></div>
                        <div class="modal-card">
                            <header class="modal-card-head">

                            </header>

                                <p>This action cannot be undone.</p>
                            </section>
                            <footer class="modal-card-foot">

                                        @click="deleteItem"

                                        :disabled="isDeleting">

                                </button>
                                <button class="button" @click="closeModal">Cancel</button>
                            </footer>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <!-- Update Price Modal -->

                        <div class="modal-background" @click="closeModal"></div>
                        <div class="modal-card">
                            <header class="modal-card-head">
                                <p class="modal-card-title">Update Price</p>

                            </header>
                            <section class="modal-card-body">
                                <p>Do you want to fetch the latest price for <span v-text="selectedItem.company"></span>?</p>

                            </section>
                            <footer class="modal-card-foot">

                                                <option 
                                                    v-for="(portfolio, index) in portfolioOptions" 
                                                    :key="index"

                                                    >
                                                    {% raw %}{{ portfolio }}{% endraw %}
                                                </option>

                                            <span class="icon"><i class="fas fa-check"></i></span>

                                        </button>
                                    </div>

                                </p>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Companies selector grouped by portfolio (scrollable) -->
                            <div class="company-list-container has-background-white" style="max-height: 400px; overflow-y: auto; padding: 0;">
                                <div v-for="(companies, portfolio) in computedGroupedCompanies" :key="portfolio" class="portfolio-section">
                                    <div class="portfolio-header is-flex is-align-items-center is-justify-content-space-between p-2 has-background-light">
                                        <h5 v-text="portfolio" class="portfolio-title is-size-5 has-text-weight-semibold has-text-dark"></h5>
                                        <div class="select-all">
                                            <label class="checkbox">
                                                <input type="checkbox" 
                                                    @change="togglePortfolio(portfolio)"
                                                    :checked="isPortfolioSelected(portfolio)">
                                                <span class="ml-1 has-text-dark">Select All</span>
                                            </label>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    
                                    <div class="company-list p-2 has-background-white">
                                        <div v-for="company in companies" :key="company.id" class="py-1 px-2 company-item" :class="{'is-selected': selectedCompanies.includes(company.id)}">
                                            <label class="checkbox is-flex is-align-items-center">
                                                <input type="checkbox" v-model="selectedCompanies" :value="company.id">
                                                <span class="ml-2 company-name has-text-dark" v-text="company.name"></span>
                                            </label>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                
                                <!-- No companies found message -->
                                <div v-if="Object.keys(computedGroupedCompanies).length === 0" class="notification is-warning">

                    </div>
